<script>
    function liveTickerHandler(initialChain = 'all') {
        return {
            sponsoredCoin: null,
            trendingCoins: [],
            isDropdownOpen: false,
            chains: [],
            selectedChainId: initialChain,
            
            get selectedChain() {
                if (!Array.isArray(this.chains)) {
                    return { id: 'all', name: 'All Chains', logo: null };
                }
                return this.chains.find(c => c.id === this.selectedChainId) || { id: 'all', name: 'All Chains', logo: null };
            },

            init() {
                if (window.location.pathname === '/') {
                    this.selectedChainId = 'all';
                }
                this.fetchData();
                setInterval(() => this.fetchData(), 90000); // Refresh every 90 seconds
            },
            selectChain(chainId) {
                if (this.selectedChainId === chainId) {
                    this.isDropdownOpen = false;
                    return;
                }
                this.selectedChainId = chainId;
                this.trendingCoins = [];
                this.sponsoredCoin = null;
                this.isDropdownOpen = false;
                this.fetchData();
            },
            async fetchData() {
                try {
                    const response = await fetch(`https://coinbazooka.com/api/live-ticker-data?chain=${this.selectedChainId}`);
                    if (!response.ok) {
                        console.error('Ticker API request failed with status:', response.status);
                        this.sponsoredCoin = null;
                        this.trendingCoins = [];
                        return;
                    }
                    const data = await response.json();
                    this.sponsoredCoin = data.sponsored_coin || null;
                    this.trendingCoins = Array.isArray(data.trending_coins) ? data.trending_coins : [];
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('Failed to fetch or parse live ticker data:', error);
                    this.sponsoredCoin = null;
                    this.trendingCoins = [];
                }
            }
        }
    }
</script>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            const swiperContainer = document.querySelector('.rotating-banner-swiper');
            if (swiperContainer) {
                const slides = swiperContainer.querySelectorAll('.swiper-slide');
                const slideCount = slides.length;
                const isLooping = slideCount > 3;
                const swiper = new Swiper(swiperContainer, {
                    loop: isLooping, 
                    slidesPerView: 1, 
                    spaceBetween: 20,
                    autoplay: { delay: 3000, disableOnInteraction: false },
                    breakpoints: {
                        768: { slidesPerView: 2, spaceBetween: 20 },
                        1024: { slidesPerView: 3, spaceBetween: 30 }
                    },
                });
            }
        });

        // ALPINE.JS CONTROLLER TERPUSAT
        function pageController() {
            return {
                // State untuk modal boost
                showBoostModal: false,
                coinId: null,
                coinName: '',
                coinImage: '',
                coinSymbol: '',
                coinBoosts: 0,
                
                // State untuk filter & sort mobile
                networkFilterOpen: false,
                sortDropdownOpen: false,
                
                get currentMilestoneBase() {
                    const boosts = parseInt(this.coinBoosts) || 0;
                    return Math.floor(boosts / 500) * 500;
                },
                get nextMilestone() {
                    return this.currentMilestoneBase + 500;
                },
                get progressInMilestone() {
                    const boosts = parseInt(this.coinBoosts) || 0;
                    return boosts - this.currentMilestoneBase;
                },
                get progressPercentage() {
                    if (this.progressInMilestone === 0 && this.coinBoosts > 0) return 0;
                    return (this.progressInMilestone / 500) * 100;
                },
                get neededForNextReward() {
                    const boosts = parseInt(this.coinBoosts) || 0;
                    return this.nextMilestone - boosts;
                },

                // Fungsi untuk membuka modal boost
                openBoostModal(id, name, image, symbol, boosts) {
                    this.coinId = id;
                    this.coinName = name;
                    this.coinImage = image;
                    this.coinSymbol = symbol;
                    this.coinBoosts = boosts;
                    this.showBoostModal = true;
                }
            }
        }
    </script>
<script>
    function searchHandler() {
        return {
            search: '',
            results: [],
            isLoading: false,
            showResults: false,
            fetchResults() {
                if (this.search.length < 2) {
                    this.results = [];
                    this.showResults = false;
                    return;
                }
                this.isLoading = true;
                this.showResults = true;

                fetch("https://coinbazooka.com/coin/api/search", {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        'X-CSRF-TOKEN': document.querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]').getAttribute('content'),
                        'Accept': 'application/json',
                    },
                    body: JSON.stringify({ value: this.search })
                })
                .then(response => response.json())
                .then(data => {
                    this.results = data.map(coin => {
                        if (coin.imageUrl) {
                            coin.image_url = coin.imageUrl.replace('/uploads/coins/', '/storage/coins/');
                        } else {
                            coin.image_url = ''; 
                        }
                        return coin;
                    });
                })
                .catch(error => console.error('Error:', error))
                .finally(() => this.isLoading = false);
            }
        }
    }
</script>

                Next
            </button>
            <button x-show="currentSlide === slides.length - 1" @click="closePopup()" class="rounded-md bg-primary px-3.5 py-2 text-sm font-semibold text-white shadow-sm hover:bg-primary/80 transition-colors">
                Explore Now
            </button>

<script>
function whatsNewPopup() {
    return {
        showPopup: false,
        currentSlide: 0,
        slides: [
            // Slide 1: The Big Leap to Web3
            {
                title: "The Alpha Drop: Welcome to CoinBazooka 2.0",
                icon: `🚀`,
                text: `<p>We've rebuilt our platform to give you an edge in the market. Connect your wallet to interact with our new Web3-integrated ecosystem and start hunting for alpha.</p>`,
                image: 'https://coinbazooka.com/assets/1.svg'
            },
            // Slide 2: Powerful New Tools
            {
                title: "Your New Coin-Hunting Toolkit",
                icon: `🛠️`,
                text: `<ul class="list-disc list-inside space-y-1">
                           <li><strong>Find Coin Early:</strong> Discover new pairs the moment they're created on-chain.</li>
                           <li><strong>Scan for Safety:</strong> Instantly check any contract for risks with our new scanner.</li>
                           <li><strong>Track Real Momentum:</strong> Our new ranking system focuses on community boosts and organic on-chain activity.</li>
                       </ul>`,
                image: 'https://coinbazooka.com/assets/2.svg'
            },
            // Slide 3: AI Coin Analyst
            {
                title: "Meet Kiara, Your AI Analyst",
                icon: `🤖`,
                text: `<p>Get instant insights on any project. Our new AI agent, Kiara, provides a summary and FAQ for every coin, giving you a unique analytical edge.</p>`,
                image: 'https://coinbazooka.com/assets/3.svg'
            },
            // Slide 4: Pro-Level Platform for Projects
            {
                title: "Launch Your Project Like a Pro",
                icon: `📈`,
                text: `<ul class="list-disc list-inside space-y-1">
                           <li><strong>Automated Campaign Dashboard:</strong> Manage and track your ads in real-time.</li>
                           <li><strong>Unlock the Golden Ticker:</strong> Get massive exposure with 500 boosts, a promoted spot, and a place in our Live Trending Ticker!</li>
                           <li><strong>Secure Web3 Payments:</strong> A seamless and secure way to manage your listings and ads.</li>
                       </ul>`,
                image: 'https://coinbazooka.com/assets/4.svg'
            },
            // Slide 5: A Brand New Experience
            {
                title: "A Faster, Sleeker Experience",
                icon: `✨`,
                text: `<p>Explore our completely revamped design, the new live trending ticker, and a faster experience on both desktop and mobile.</p>`,
                image: 'https://coinbazooka.com/assets/5.svg'
            }
        ],
        init() {
            // Periksa apakah pengguna sudah melihat pop-up ini sebelumnya
            if (localStorage.getItem('hasSeenV2Update') !== 'true') {
                // Tampilkan setelah 2 detik
                setTimeout(() => {
                    this.showPopup = true;
                }, 2000);
            }
        },
        nextSlide() {
            if (this.currentSlide < this.slides.length - 1) {
                this.currentSlide++;
            }
        },
        closePopup() {
            this.showPopup = false;
            // Tandai bahwa pengguna sudah melihat pop-up ini
            localStorage.setItem('hasSeenV2Update', 'true');
        }
    }
}
</script>
